 dosti ko lekar chaunkaane vaali yah ghatana hyderabad kii he

 cybrabad police ne desh ke vyastatam airporton main se ek hyderabad ke rajeev gandhi international airport ko bam kii dhamkee bharaa mail bhejne vaale ko giraftaar kar liya

 Arun Jaitley Passes Away: Former Union Minister and senior BJP leader Arun Jaitley died on Saturday in AIIMS
 vah 66 varsh ke the
 Jaitley was undergoing treatment at AIIMS for several weeks
 ames ne isaki ghoshnaa karte hue ek sankshipt bayaan main kaha ki ham bade dukh ke saath arun jetali ke nidhan kii jaankaree de rahe hai
 Jaitley was admitted to the All India Institute of Medical Sciences (AIIMS) here on August 9 after complaining of difficulty in breathing and discomfort
 chaatr jivan main hi bhrashtachar ke khilaaf sangharsh karne vaale arun jetali ne vitt mantralay, corporate maamle ke mantralay, soochna evam prasaaran mantralay, kanoon mantralay or raksha mantralay sambhala
 Wherever he stayed, he continued to receive appreciation
 bataa den, arun jetali charted acountint bananaa chaahate the
 But the father's profession chose advocacy
 is dauraan unhone boforce ghotaale kii jaanch kii tafasil taiyaar kii thi
 Jaitley presented documents on the subject of 'corruption and Crime in India' before the Indian British Legal Court
 june 1998 main nashile padaarthon kii taskari par roak lagane ke liye antarrashtriya kanoon ko adhiniyamit karne ke uddeshy se yojit sanyukt raashtra sangh sammelan main ve bharat sarkaar ke pratinidhi ke taur par shaamil hue the
 Jaitley wrote several books on legal and contemporary problems
 laalkrishna adwani, madhavrao sindhiya samet kai varisht netaa arun jetali ke client rahe hai
 He served as the Leader of the Opposition in the Rajya Sabha from 2009 to 2014
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ke netritv vaali sarkaar main 26 may 2014 ko arun jetali ko vitt mantri banaaya gaya
 He was also given the charge of Ministry of Corporate Affairs and Ministry of Defense
 ve 27 may 2014 se 14 may 2018 tak kendriya vitt evam corporate maamalon ke mantri rahe
 He also held the charge of the Ministry of Defense from 27 May 2014 to 9 November 2014
 ve 13 march 2017 se 3 sitambar 2017 tak raksha mantri ke pad par rahe

 'mad about dance' main dance ke junun ke alaava dosti nibhaane ke achche jazbe hai

 chote-chote tukdon main dance ke kai forms hai, jaise loking, popping, brake dance, free style dance aadi
 
 
 But despite being based on dance, the film lacks dance
 dance kaa junun to he, magar compatishan ke teen se chaar tukdon main dance dikhaaya gaya he
 Good music is also necessary for dancing, in that sense the music of the film is weak
 dance compatishan jeetne or group banane kii jaddojahad he, magar kahani bahut hi dhimi he
 Passion recalled another thing that just as the film's character Aarav seems to have an attachment to dance, Sahil Prem, who plays this character, had a similar desire to make a film on dance

 Although it is a documentary film, it has been released as a feature film
 
 
 yah documentry bataati he ki kaise mumbai se 300 kilometre dur maalegaanv shahar main 'maalegaanv kaa superman' naam kii film banaai gai thi, jisamen hollywood kii superman filmon kaa mazaaq udaaya gaya tha
 
 
 Director Faiza Ahmed filmed this documentary during the shooting of 'malegaon Ka Superman', which showed the film industry of Malegaon, small, poor, far away from technology and facilities, but these problems are 'malegaon Superman The director of 'sheikh Nasir, Writer Farog Jaffrey and the rest of the team are not able to break the spirits, and these people shoot their film on Handycam
 
 
 tippaniyan In this documentary, learn how Shafiq, a laborer of the powerloom industry, takes a leave and plays Superman, who was not due to cancer last year
 
 
 jis dhang se maalegaanv vaale rickshaw, motorcycle, trollies or khambhe kii madad se apane superman ko hawa main udaate hai, use dekhakar aap hansate-hansate lotpot ho jaaenge
 
 
 The man also plays Superman, and carries the stuff of his film team
 
 
 aap yah bhi janenge ki kaise maalegaanv kii filmon main ladakon ko ladakiyon ke role karne padate hai
 
 
 Interestingly, while the original film 'malegaon Ka Superman' was made for just one lakh rupees, the documentary 'superman of Malegaon' made on its making is made for Rs 24 lakhs
 
 
 'superman of maalegaanv' cinema students or filmameking main dilchaspee rakhane waalon ke liye to he hi, isse bhi zyada aam aadmi ke liye dekhne laayak he film banane ko lekar maalegaanv waalon kaa jajba
 
 
 Our rating for 'superman of Malegaon' is - 3 stars
 
 
 diarector faiza ahamed ne apni yah documentry 'maalegaanv kaa superman' kii shooting ke dauraan hi filmai thi, jisamen maalegaanv kii, choti-si, garib, takanic or suvidhaon se koson dur film industry dikhaai gai he, lekin ye museebataan film 'maalegaanv kaa superman' ke diarector shaikh nasir, riter farogh jaafaree or baaki team kaa hausala nahin tod paatin, or ye log handycam par apni film shoot karte hai
 
 
 The comments is documentry main jaaniye ki kaise powerloom industry kaa majdoor shafik chuttee lekar superman kaa role karata he, jo pichley saal cancer kii vajah se nahin rahaa
 
 
 Seeing the manner in which Malegaon blows his Superman in the air with the help of rickshaws, motorcycles, trolleys and poles, you will be amused
 
 
 yah shaks superman kaa role bhi karata he, or apni film team kaa saamaan bhi dhota he
 
 
 You will also learn how in Malegaon movies, boys have to play girls
 
 
 dilachasp baat yah he ki jahaan original film 'maalegaanv kaa superman' sirf ek lakh rupee main ban gai thi, vahiin uski mekking par bani yah documentry 'superman of maalegaanv' 24 lakh rupee main bani he
